\documentclass{article}

\usepackage{standalone}
\usepackage{tikz}
\usepackage{amsmath,amssymb}
\usepackage{subcaption}
\usepackage{fmtcount}
\usetikzlibrary{calc, patterns, intersections}

\usepackage{graphicx}
\usepackage{multicol}
\usepackage{import}

\usepackage{pgfplots}
\pgfplotsset{compat=1.17}

\newcommand{\lineinput}[1]{\begingroup\endlinechar=-1 \input{#1}\endgroup}

\tikzset{
	hatch distance/.store in=\hatchdistance,
	hatch distance=10pt,
	hatch thickness/.store in=\hatchthickness,
	hatch thickness=2pt
}

\makeatletter
\pgfdeclarepatternformonly[\hatchdistance,\hatchthickness]{flexible hatch}
{\pgfqpoint{-\hatchdistance}{-\hatchdistance}}%0pt
{\pgfqpoint{2\hatchdistance}{2\hatchdistance}}
{\pgfpoint{\hatchdistance}{\hatchdistance}}%{\hatchdistance-1pt}{\hatchdistance-1pt}}%
{
	\pgfsetcolor{\tikz@pattern@color}
	\pgfsetlinewidth{\hatchthickness}
	\pgfpathmoveto{\pgfqpoint{\hatchdistance}{-\hatchdistance}}%\pgfqpoint{0pt}{0pt}}
	\pgfpathlineto{\pgfqpoint{-\hatchdistance}{\hatchdistance}}%\pgfqpoint{\hatchdistance}{\hatchdistance}}
	\pgfusepath{stroke}
}
\makeatother

\graphicspath{{../2020.11.10. Sorting Algorithm 310. Take 2/clipart/}{./images/}}
